    var redirectToSubnavIfAuthenticated = "false";
    var redirectToHomeIfAnonymous = "false";
    var subNavPath = "https://www.lq.com/en/findandbook/new-openings.html";
    var homePath = "https://www.lq.com/en.html";
    	
	if (LQcom.Session.ReturnsUserProfile.isLoggedIn()) {
    	if (redirectToSubnavIfAuthenticated == "true" && window.location != subNavPath) {
    		LQcom.ready(function () {window.location.replace(subNavPath);});
  		}
	} 
	else {
    	if (redirectToHomeIfAnonymous == "true" && window.location != homePath) {
    		LQcom.ready(function () {window.location.replace(homePath);});
    	}
	}

<script type="text/javascript">


    $(".about-lq-li:last-child span").addClass("removeRightBorder");

    $(".about-lq-li").click(function (event) {

        // Check if the itemclicked data attribute availabel for the current element
        var itemclicked = $(this).data("itemclicked");


        if (typeof(itemclicked) == 'undefined' || itemclicked == 'false') {

            //First time item is clicked. Adding itemclicked data attribute to the current item
            $(this).data("itemclicked", "true");

            if ($(this).find(('ul li')).length > 0) {
                // Preventing the default click event, to open the drop down
                event.preventDefault();

                $(this).find('span').addClass("hoverClass");
                $(this).find('ul').css("visibility", "visible");

                var eleTest = $(this).prev();
                $(eleTest.find("span")).addClass("removeRightBorder");


            }
        }


    });

    $(".about-lq-li").mouseleave(function (event) {

        $(this).data("itemclicked", 'false');

        $(this).find('span').removeClass("hoverClass");

        $(this).find('ul').css("visibility", "hidden");

        var eleTest = $(this).prev();
        $(eleTest.find("span")).removeClass("removeRightBorder");

    });

</script>

<script>
LQcom.ready(function() {
	if (LQcom.Session.ReturnsUserProfile.isLoggedIn()) {
		$(".hideWhenAnon").removeClass("hide").addClass("notHidden");
	} else {
		$(".hideWhenAuth").removeClass("hide").addClass("notHidden");
	}
	$(".subNavList").each(function(){
		if(!$(this).hasClass("hide")){
			$(this).children().each(function(){
				if(!$(this).hasClass("hide")){
					$(this).css("border-left","none");
					return false;
				}
			});
			$($(this).children().get().reverse()).each(function() {
				if(!$(this).hasClass("hide")){
					$(this).css("border-right","none");
					return false;
				}
			});
		}
	});
});
</script></div>

<script>

	$(".signInModule").on("keyup", function (event) {
		if (event.which == 13) {
			$(".formLinks #btnSignIn").trigger('click');
		}
	});
    $(lqloginsreturnsetup);
    function lqloginsreturnsetup() {
        var globalData = LQcom.Session.Global.getData();
        $('#loginPageSessionId').val(globalData.sessionId);

        if (globalData.rememberMe == "Y") {
            $("#remember").attr("checked", "checked");
        }

        $("#remember").change(function() {
            if ($(this).is(':checked')) {
                globalData.rememberMe = "Y";
            } else {
                globalData.rememberMe = "N";
            }
            LQcom.Session.Global.record(globalData);
        });

    
        if ($.cookie("returnsid") && $("#remember").is(':checked')) {
            $("#returnsid").val($.cookie("returnsid"));
        }
    
        watermark("returnsid", "Email or Member #");
        $('#passwordWatermark').focus(function() {
            $('#passwordWatermark').hide();
            $('#password').show().focus();
        });
        $("#password").blur(function() {
            if ($('#password').val() == '') {
                $('#passwordWatermark').show();
                $('#password').hide();
            }
        });
        $("#frgtpwd").attr("href", "/content/lq/lq-com/en/popups/forgot-password.html");


        $("#forgotpassword").fancybox({
            'autoSize': false,
            'width': 780,
            'height': 500,
            'autoScale': false,
            'transitionIn': 'none',
            'transitionOut': 'none',
            'type': 'iframe'
        });

        $(".btnSignIn").click(function() {
     		 var x = $("#returnsid").val();
            var atpos = x.indexOf("@");
            var dotpos = x.lastIndexOf(".");
            var flag = 0;
            var emailCheck = true;
           if (atpos< 1 || dotpos<atpos+2 || dotpos+2>=x.length) {
                   emailCheck = false;
                   flag=1;
   		 	}
           if(atpos >= 0 && flag ==1){
           	LQcom.ReturnsLogin.showErrorPanel("The email address you entered is not valid, please enter a valid email address to log into your account.");
           	return;
           }
			if(!$(this).hasClass("disabled")){
	        	$(this).addClass("disabled");
	            var returnsLoginAction = $("#rcCheckAccountForm").attr('action');
	            //Adding to check that if its email id, don't do uppercase
				if(!emailCheck){
					$("#returnsid").val($("#returnsid").val().toUpperCase());
				}
				//Check and added functionality ends here
	            if ($("#remember").is(':checked')) {
	            	//TODO to add the condition to add cookie variable on basis of email or returns id
	            	$.cookie('returnsid', $("#returnsid").val(), {'path': '/', expires: 365});	
	            } else {
	            	$.removeCookie('returnsid', {'path': '/'});	
	            }
			}
            $("#errmsg").html("");
            var formData = $("#rcCheckAccountForm").serialize();
            LQcom.ReturnsLogin.loginUser(returnsLoginAction, formData);  
       });
    }
    
</script>

<script>
    LQcom.googleMaps.loadGoogleMapsLib = true;
    LQcom.ready(function() {
        LQcom.googleMaps.initGeoCoder();
        
        var ccSearch = LQcom.Session.FindAndBook.getData();
        var ccSession = LQcom.Session.Global.getData();
        
        if(ccSearch.checkinDate){
        $('#checkInDate').val(ccSearch.checkinDate);
        }
        if(ccSearch.checkoutDate){
        $('#checkOutDate').val(ccSearch.checkoutDate);
        }
        if(ccSearch.promoCode){
        $('#promoCode').val(ccSearch.promoCode);
        }

        if(ccSearch.rateType){
        $('select[name=specialRates]').val(ccSearch.rateType);
        }

        if(ccSearch.rooms){
        if(ccSearch.rooms != "")
        	$('select[name=rooms]').val(ccSearch.rooms);
        }
        if(ccSearch.adults){
        if(ccSearch.adults != "")
        	$('select[name=adults]').val(ccSearch.adults);
        }
        if(ccSearch.children){
        if(ccSearch.children != "")
       		$('select[name=numChildren]').val(ccSearch.children);
        }

        if(ccSearch.searchRadius){
        if(ccSearch.searchRadius != "" && typeof ccSearch.searchRadius != 'undefined')
        	$('select[name=searchRadius]').val(ccSearch.searchRadius);
        }
        
        if(ccSession.sessionId){
        if(ccSession.sessionId != "" && typeof ccSession.sessionId != 'undefined')
        	$('input[name=sessionId]').val(ccSession.sessionId);
        }
        
        
        $("#checkInDate").blur(function(){
			var dt = $("#checkInDate").val();
            if(!LQcom.isDateValid(dt)){
                alert("The Check-In Date and Check-Out Date must be in MM/DD/YYYY format. Please enter your dates in this format or select dates from the graphical Calendar that appears when you click into each field.");
                $("#checkInDate").val(LQcom.checkPreceedingZeroForDate(LQcom.formatDate(LQcom.Defaults.arrivalDate)));
                $("#checkOutDate").val(LQcom.checkPreceedingZeroForDate(LQcom.formatDate(LQcom.Defaults.departureDate)));
            }

        });

        $("#checkOutDate").blur(function(){
			var dt = $("#checkOutDate").val();
            if(!LQcom.isDateValid(dt)){
                alert("The Check-In Date and Check-Out Date must be in MM/DD/YYYY format. Please enter your dates in this format or select dates from the graphical Calendar that appears when you click into each field.");
                $("#checkInDate").val(LQcom.checkPreceedingZeroForDate(LQcom.formatDate(LQcom.Defaults.arrivalDate)));
                $("#checkOutDate").val(LQcom.checkPreceedingZeroForDate(LQcom.formatDate(LQcom.Defaults.departureDate)));
            }

        });
        
    });
</script>

                        <script>

                            LQcom.datePicker.createDatePicker("checkInDate", "checkOutDate", "en");
                            
                            function codeAddress(form) {
                                LQcom.findHotels.clearError();
                                
                                var address = "";
                                if (form.searchAddress.value != '')
                                    address += form.searchAddress.value + " ";
                                address += form.searchCity.value + " ";
                                address += form.searchState.value + " ";
                                if (form.searchPostal.value != '')
                                    address += form.searchPostal.value + " ";

                                if ((form.searchCity.value == '' || typeof form.searchState == 'undefined') && form.searchPostal.value == '') {
                                    var errDiv = document.getElementById('errmsg');
                                    errDiv.innerHTML += '<div class="message error"><li>Please specify a "City" & "State" or "Zip" to continue your search</li></div>';
                                } else if (LQcom.googleMaps.geocoder) {
                                    address = LQcom.findHotels.filterAddress(address); // 8063
                                    LQcom.googleMaps.geocoder.geocode({'address': address}, function(results, status) {
                                        if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                                            var point = results[0].geometry.location;
                                            form.lat.value = point.lat();
                                            form.lon.value = point.lng();
                                            form.stateAndCountryCode.value = $("#searchState :selected").text()+", "+form.searchCountryCode.value;

                                            LQcom.findHotels.updateContext(form, LQcom.findHotels.codeLocationByAddress);
                                            form.submit();
                                        } else {
                                            var errDiv = document.getElementById('errmsg');
                                            errDiv.innerHTML += '<div class="message error"><li>Requested location not found</li></div>';

                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                                
                            }
                            
                            LQcom.ready(function () {
                            	var globalData = LQcom.Session.Global.getData();
                            	
                            	$.get("/content/lq/lq-com/en/navigation/findandbook/jcr:content/main-content/tabs/tab_1/findhotelbyaddress.destinations.html?sessionId=" +  globalData.sessionId, function(data) {
                            		var destinationsByAddress = LQcom.parseJSON(data);
                                	$('#searchCity').autocomplete({
                                	    lookup: destinationsByAddress,
                                	    width:'230px',
                                		lookupFilter: function (suggestion, originalQuery, queryLowerCase) {
                                	    	return suggestion.value.toLowerCase().match("^"+queryLowerCase);
                                	    },
                                		formatResult:function(suggestion, currentValue){
                                			return suggestion.value;
                                		},
                                		onSelect: function (suggestion) {
                                			var values = suggestion.data.split(",");
                                			$(this).val(values[0]);
                                			$("#searchState").val(values[1]);
                                			$("#searchCountryCode").val(values[2]);
                                		}
                                	});
                            	});
                            });


                        </script>
</div>

<script>
    LQcom.ready(function () {
        var ccSearch = LQcom.Session.FindAndBook.getData();
        var ccSession = LQcom.Session.Global.getData();
        
        if(ccSession.sessionId){
            if(ccSession.sessionId != "" && typeof ccSession.sessionId != 'undefined')
            	$('input[name=sessionId]').val(ccSession.sessionId);
        }
        
        $('#route_indate').val(ccSearch.checkinDate);
        $('#route_outdate').val(ccSearch.checkoutDate);
        
        $('input[name=promoCode]').val(ccSearch.promoCode);
        $('input[name=specialRates]').val(ccSearch.rateType);

        if(ccSearch.searchRadius != "" && typeof ccSearch.searchRadius != 'undefined') 
        	$('select[name=searchRadius]').val(ccSearch.searchRadius);

        var globalData = LQcom.Session.Global.getData();
        
       	$.get("/content/lq/lq-com/en/navigation/findandbook/jcr:content/main-content/tabs/tab_3/findhotelbyroute.destinations.html?sessionId=" +  globalData.sessionId, function(data) {
       		var destinationsbyRoute=LQcom.parseJSON(data);
           	$('#searchOCity, #searchDCity').autocomplete({
           	    lookup: destinationsbyRoute,
           	    width:'228',
           		lookupFilter: function (suggestion, originalQuery, queryLowerCase) {
           	    	return suggestion.value.toLowerCase().match("^"+queryLowerCase);
           	    },
           		formatResult:function(suggestion, currentValue){
           			return suggestion.value;
           		},
           		onSelect: function (suggestion) {
           			var values = suggestion.data.split(",");
           			$(this).val(values[0]);
           			if($(this).attr("id").indexOf("searchOCity") != -1){
           				$("#searchOState").val(values[1]);
           			}else{
           				$("#searchDState").val(values[1]);
           			}
           		}
           	});
       	});

    });
    
    function findHotelsByRoute(form, errNF, errZR, errIR, errQL, errRD, errUE, errCO, errCD, errSO, errSD, errSA) {
    	LQcom.findHotels.getRouteCoords(form, errNF, errZR, errIR, errQL, errRD, errUE, errCO, errCD, errSO, errSD, errSA);
			
    }
</script>

<script>

    LQcom.ready(function() {
        var source = $("#attraction-results-template").html();
        var template = Handlebars.compile(source);
        var frm = document.getElementById("multiSearchForm");
        $("#submitFindByAttraction").click(function() {
            recordClientContext(frm);
            LQcom.googleMaps.findByAttraction($("#searchPlace").val());
        });
        
    	$('#searchPlace').keypress(function(e){
    		var code = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
    	    if(code == 13)
    	    {
    	    	$("#submitFindByAttraction").click();
                return false;
    	        
    	    }
    	});
    	
        LQcom.googleMaps.findByAttraction = function(txtQuery) {
            var request = {
                query: txtQuery
            };
            LQcom.googleMaps.placesSearch.textSearch(request, LQcom.googleMaps.findByAttractionCallback);

        };
        LQcom.googleMaps.findByAttractionCallback = function(results, status) {
            LQcom.googleMaps.attractionResults = [];
            if (status === google.maps.places.PlacesServiceStatus.OK) {
                var iLen = 8;
                var place;
                if (results.length < 8) {
                    iLen = results.length;
                }


                for (var i = 0; i < iLen; i++) {
                    place = results[i];
                    LQcom.googleMaps.attractionResults.push({"name": place.name, "formatted_address": place.formatted_address, "lat": place.geometry.location.lat(), "lng": place.geometry.location.lng()});
                }
                var context = {"results": LQcom.googleMaps.attractionResults};

                if (iLen > 1) {
                    $("#maincontainer").html(template(context));
                } else {
                    $("#singleResult").html(template(context));
                }

                var ccSearch = LQcom.Session.FindAndBook.getData();
                $('#multi_result_indate').val(ccSearch.checkinDate);
                $('#multi_result_outdate').val(ccSearch.checkoutDate);
                $('input[name=promoCode]').val(ccSearch.promoCode);
                $('input[name=specialRates]').val(ccSearch.rateType);
                $('input[name=searchRadius]').val(ccSearch.searchRadius);
                $('input[name=bookingPage]').val(ccSearch.bookingPage);
               
              //  $('input[name=searchCity]').val($("#searchPlace").val());
                if (iLen === 1) {
                    $(".singleResult").click();
                }
            }
        };
    });
</script></div>

</div>

                    </div>
                
            </div>

        </div>

<script>
    LQcom.ready(function() {
        /**delimited links**/
        var wdth = 0;
        $(".delimitedlinks").each(function(i) {

            wdth = $(this).width();

            var w = 0;

            $(this).find("ul li").each(function(idx, li) {
                var item = $(li);

                w = w + item.outerWidth();
                if (w >= wdth) {
                    w = item.outerWidth();
                    // item.css("border-left","none");
                    item.find("a").each(function(idx, a) {
                        var $a = $(a);
                        $a.css("padding-left", "0px");
                        $a.css("margin-left", "0px");
                    });
                    item.prev().remove();
                }


            });

        });
        /**delimited links**/

    });
</script>
